          --mr-toggled-font-family: inherit;
          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-open-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[issueClosed] {
          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }
        .container-issue-content {
          padding: 0;
          flex-grow: 1;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: space-between;
          flex-direction: row;
          flex-wrap: nowrap;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          padding-top: 0.5em;
        }
        .container-outside {
          box-sizing: border-box;
          width: 100%;
          max-width: 100%;
          margin: auto;
          padding: 0;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: space-between;
          flex-direction: row;
          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }
        .container-no-issue {
          padding: 0.5em 16px;
          font-size: var(--chops-large-font-size);
        }
        .metadata-container {
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          background: var(--monorail-metadata-toggled-bg);
          border-right: var(--chops-normal-border);
          border-bottom: var(--chops-normal-border);
          width: 24em;
          min-width: 256px;
          flex-grow: 0;
          flex-shrink: 0;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          z-index: 100;
        }
        .issue-header-container {
          z-index: 10;
          position: sticky;
          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          margin-bottom: 0.25em;
          width: 100%;
        }
        mr-issue-details {
          min-width: 50%;
          max-width: 1000px;
          flex-grow: 1;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          min-height: 100%;
          padding-left: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);
          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);
        }
        mr-issue-metadata {
          position: sticky;
          overflow-y: auto;
          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }
        mr-launch-overview {
          border-left: var(--chops-normal-border);
          padding-left: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);
          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);
          flex-grow: 0;
          flex-shrink: 0;
          width: 50%;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          min-height: 100%;
        }
        @media (max-width: 1126px) {
          .container-issue-content {
            flex-direction: column;
            padding: 0 var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);
          }
          mr-issue-details, mr-launch-overview {
            width: 100%;
            padding: 0;
            border: 0;
          }
        }
        @media (max-width: 840px) {

          .metadata-container {

            position: static;
          }
        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

And, if the first arg of `base::BarrierClosure` is zero, it will run the callback directly(2).



<span class="line"><!---->And, if the first arg of `base::BarrierClosure` is zero, it will run the callback directly(2).<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->RepeatingClosure BarrierClosure(size_t num_callbacks_left,<!----></span>



<br>





                                OnceClosure done_closure) {



<span class="line"><!---->                                OnceClosure done_closure) {<!----></span>



<br>





  if (num_callbacks_left == 0) {  // =>(1)



<span class="line"><!---->  if (num_callbacks_left == 0) {  // =&gt;(1)<!----></span>



<br>





    std::move(done_closure).Run();



<span class="line"><!---->    std::move(done_closure).Run();<!----></span>



<br>





    return BindRepeating(&ShouldNeverRun);



<span class="line"><!---->    return BindRepeating(&amp;ShouldNeverRun);<!----></span>



<br>





  }



<span class="line"><!---->  }<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  return BindRepeating(&BarrierInfo::Run,



<span class="line"><!---->  return BindRepeating(&amp;BarrierInfo::Run,<!----></span>



<br>





                       std::make_unique<BarrierInfo>(num_callbacks_left,



<span class="line"><!---->                       std::make_unique&lt;BarrierInfo&gt;(num_callbacks_left,<!----></span>



<br>





                                                     std::move(done_closure)));



<span class="line"><!---->                                                     std::move(done_closure)));<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





So, if we delete the note, the size of `notes_added_` in (3) is zero, So the callback `OnFrameChangesApplied` will be called directly, which will erase the `FrameUserNoteChanges` from the map and delete it. When `notes_added_` is used to enter the for loop, UAF occurs.



<span class="line"><!---->So, if we delete the note, the size of `notes_added_` in (3) is zero, So the callback `OnFrameChangesApplied` will be called directly, which will erase the `FrameUserNoteChanges` from the map and delete it. When `notes_added_` is used to enter the for loop, UAF occurs.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





To trigger this code path(call `UserNoteService::OnNoteModelsFetched`), you could dup the same tab that has been added any notes OR you could just refresh the tab that has any notes. So the poc could be simplified by refreshing the tab and don't need to open another same tab.



<span class="line"><!---->To trigger this code path(call `UserNoteService::OnNoteModelsFetched`), you could dup the same tab that has been added any notes OR you could just refresh the tab that has any notes. So the poc could be simplified by refreshing the tab and don't need to open another same tab.<!----></span>

For some reason I am unable to repro this. Even when notes_added_.size() == 0 in the FrameUserNoteChanges, somehow everything works just fine for me on Windows. These two unit tests [1] [2] also exercise this exact code path (notes_added_.size() == 0) on all platforms and they pass just fine.



<span class="line"><!---->For some reason I am unable to repro this. Even when notes_added_.size() == 0 in the FrameUserNoteChanges, somehow everything works just fine for me on Windows. These two unit tests [1] [2] also exercise this exact code path (notes_added_.size() == 0) on all platforms and they pass just fine.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I guess it doesn't hurt to add an explicit check for notes_added_.empty() and invoke the callback and return before the for loop, but since I don't have a repro I'm not able to confirm this fixes the issue you're seeing. I'll send a CL shortly!



<span class="line"><!---->I guess it doesn't hurt to add an explicit check for notes_added_.empty() and invoke the callback and return before the for loop, but since I don't have a repro I'm not able to confirm this fixes the issue you're seeing. I'll send a CL shortly!<!----></span>

[Notes] Tentatively fix crash in FrameUserNoteChanges::Apply



<span class="line"><!---->[Notes] Tentatively fix crash in FrameUserNoteChanges::Apply<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When there's a note change in a page with only modified and / or



<span class="line"><!---->When there's a note change in a page with only modified and / or<!----></span>



<br>





deleted notes (notes_added_.size() == 0), FrameUserNoteChanges::Apply



<span class="line"><!---->deleted notes (notes_added_.size() == 0), FrameUserNoteChanges::Apply<!----></span>



<br>





crashes. This is because the callback it's passed destroys the



<span class="line"><!---->crashes. This is because the callback it's passed destroys the<!----></span>



<br>





FrameUserNoteChanges instance, and when there are no added notes in the



<span class="line"><!---->FrameUserNoteChanges instance, and when there are no added notes in the<!----></span>



<br>





change, the BarrierClosure used by Apply immediately invokes the



<span class="line"><!---->change, the BarrierClosure used by Apply immediately invokes the<!----></span>



<br>





callback. By the time the next line (the loop) attempts to iterate



<span class="line"><!---->callback. By the time the next line (the loop) attempts to iterate<!----></span>



<br>





notes_added_, the instance has already been destroyed.



<span class="line"><!---->notes_added_, the instance has already been destroyed.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The fix is simply to return early if there are no added notes.



<span class="line"><!---->The fix is simply to return early if there are no added notes.<!----></span>



<br>





Unfortunately I cannot repro the crash in my dev environment, so this



<span class="line"><!---->Unfortunately I cannot repro the crash in my dev environment, so this<!----></span>



<br>





fix cannot be verified. However, this code path is covered by unit tests



<span class="line"><!---->fix cannot be verified. However, this code path is covered by unit tests<!----></span>



<br>





(which oddly also weren't affected by the crash).



<span class="line"><!---->(which oddly also weren't affected by the crash).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.<!----></span>

 with any questions.

Target project:

<label for="targetProjectInput">Target project:</label>


            


              

<input id="targetProjectInput" aria-owns="chops-autocomplete-1" aria-autocomplete="both" aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="listbox" aria-activedescendant="">


              




      


        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
